04 Nov 2016 04:05:51 : LimitlessMc, botchat, Gerald#7099, ​
Hello, I am Gerald, the channel Bot. I can do many things, I can even be extended by plugins (weehee).

Current commands: (note that arguments in <> are required, those in [] not)
  - !clean  : lets me purge messages, options below
    - !clean lets me purge the last 50 messages
    - !clean <number> does the same for n messages (no maximum :P)
    - !clean infinite removes messages until !kill, even the end of the channel doesn't seem like the limit
    - !clean images deletes any message containing either a link to a jpg, !meme or an attachment
    - !clean <string> removes every message containing the string
    - !clean @someone cleans @someones messages in the last 100
  - !help (!info) : Prints the help
  - !kill : Kills me and lets me (hopefully) respawn instantly
  - !ping (!pong) : Ping Pong
  - (DM) !nobroadcast : Disables update broadcasts from me if you have a server
  - (DM) !dobroadcast : Enables update broadcasts from me again
  - !bugreport <message> : File a bug so it will reach my master even if you can't contact him directly (If it's abused, I will block certain ~~ab~~users)
  - !invite : Add me to your server
  - !status : Prints some overall status
  - !plugins : Prints informations about all plugins
  - (DM) !dropbox <secret> : Register Dropbox. Go to https://ultramc.org:8087/dropbox/authorize
  - !id <beginning of name> : Outputs their internal id
  - !serverid : Prints this server's id
  - !channelid : Let me output the id of thid channel
  - !roleids : Lists all roles with their ids
  - !mention <role name> : Mentions everyone in that role
  - !permissions <username> : Lists all permissions the spefific user has in this channel
  - !meme <text you wanna write> : Generate a funny image
  - !pause : Pauses playback
  - !stop : Stops playback and empties the queue
  - !queue : Prints the current queue
  - !shufflequeue : Shuffles the queue
  - !flushqueue : Empties the queue
04 Nov 2016 04:05:52 : LimitlessMc, botchat, Gerald#7099, ​
  - !skip : Skips the current song
  - !replay : Adds the current playing song to the queue
  - !webplayer : Outputs your personal webplayer url
  - !resetsecret : Resets your webplayer secret in case you lost it
  - !soundcloud <name> : Plays a specific song from soundcloud
  - !youtube <name> : Plays a specific song from youtube. Can also be a url
  - !stats  : Outputs which users wrote the most in this channel
  - !words  : Outputs which users wrote the most words in this channel
  - !topwords  : Sends the most common words in this channel
  - !suspicious  : NSA-like who should be tracked a bit more :)
  - !weblog  : The channel's weblog for easy search in the browser
  - !punchcard  : The channel's punchcard - when are people active in here
  - (DM) !steam Authenticates a steam user linking his steam id to the discord id (visit https://ultramc.org:8087/steam
  - (DM) !nosteam Deauthenticates a steam user and disables notifications
  - (DM) !arkserver <name> : Creates an api token for use of the ARK webalarms
  - (DM) !deleteark <key> : Delete an ARK server from the config. Provide the key as argument
  - !rate [@mention] : outputs my rating for a user
  - !luck [@mention] : outputs the luck of a user today

(DM) means that you have to issue this command via a direct message to me.

04 Nov 2016 19:09:31 : The Wild Weebs, coding, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```Question 1.
First lets define a Base-Case for this problem. We can say when the length of the array is 1, we simply return that number.
The recursion itself will consist of 2 recursive calls, and 1 call to a 'helper' method.
Lets define the Helper method first. This method will find the largest Substring that includes a specific index of the array, going as far as a given max and min index.
The way this will work is it will calculate the maximum sum going left and the maximum sum going right. It will find these subsequences using 1 for loop each, and keep track of the current sum of numbers.
The Call to this Helper method would be simply the array, the lowest index, the mid index, and the max index. (The Mid index will be used as the specific index the substring has to include)
The 2 recursive calls in the main method would simply be calling the method using the mid index instead of the max index. (This will find the max subsequence of the left half) and a similar thing for the right half, replacing the min index with mid+1.

And the final return will be the max of these 3 values.
Here is what it will look in code form:
mid = (min + max)/2
return Max(    SubSequence(list, min, mid),
        SubSequence(list, mid + 1, max),
        Helper(list, min, mid, max)

For example, if the array was 1, -3, 2, 5, -5, 5, 1, we would have these calls to the Helper method.
1, -3, 2, 5, -5, 5, 1 | 1, -3, 2, 5 | -5, 5, 1 | 1, -3 | 2, 5 | -5, 5 | 1 | 1 | -3 | 2 | 5 | -5 | 5 | 
and the final return will be the MAX value of all of these, which in this case is from the 1st call, as the max array is [2, 5, -5, 5, 1]```

04 Nov 2016 19:57:42 : The Wild Weebs, coding, FinaldF#5864, Root r = x(length of array x / 2)
r cost is equal to max weight of cost in array c 
remove weight given to x from cost 
while there is an x not in BST 
    Build BST by adding x(length/2) then removing it from the array
    Max = 0 
    for I until length of c
        if max < c(i)
            max = c(i)
        end if
    end for
    add c as x weight where x is the node just added to the BST
    remove c value from the array
end while
return tree.

04 Nov 2016 20:30:12 : The Wild Weebs, coding, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```Part B
== Psuedocode ==
Def FindSequence(Sequence)
IF number of Segments in Sequence equals 1
    return Sequence
END IF
For Every Segement in Sequence
    Group_With_Left = The Sequence with (Segment and Segment to the Left merged)
    Group_With_Right = The Sequence with (Segment and Segment to the Right merged)
    No_change = cost2(Sequence,Sequence) 
    Left = cost2(Sequence, FindSequence(Group_With_Left))
    Right = cost2(Sequence, FindSequence(Group_With_Right))
    Return the Sequence, either the Original, Group_With_Left, or Group_With_Right, depending on the min value of cost2
END FOR```

04 Nov 2016 20:40:07 : The Wild Weebs, coding, enragednuke#2565, https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=062VW-wQrD0&feature=youtu.be
04 Nov 2016 20:40:59 : The Wild Weebs, coding, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```== Psuedocode ==
Def FindSequence(Sequence)
    IF number of Segments in Sequence equals 1
        return Sequence
    END IF
    FOR Every Segment in Sequence
        Group_With_Left = The Sequence If you merged Segment and the Segment to the Left
        Group_With_Right = The Sequence If you merged Segment and the Segment to the Right
        No_change = cost2(Sequence,Sequence)
        Left = cost2(Sequence, FindSequence(Group_With_Left))
        Right = cost2(Sequence, FindSequence(Group_With_Right))
        IF min(No_change, Left, Right) = No_change
            return Sequence
        ELSE IF min(No_change, Left, Right) = Left
            return Group_With_Left
        ELSE
            return Group_With_Right
        END IF
    END FOR
END FUNC

Def cost2(Sequence1, Sequence2)
    cost = 0
    FOR X in range(0, Sequence1.length-1, 1)
        cost += (Sequence1[X] - Sequence2[X])^2
    END FOR
    FOR every Segment in Sequence2
        cost -= (Segment.length)^2
    END FOR
    return cost
END FUNC```
